Flipt Release Notes\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\n> These changes require action from users upgrading.\n\n### **Pagination API**: Offset-based pagination removed in favor of cursor-based pagination\n\n- **Component**: List operations (flags, segments, rules, namespaces)\n- **Impact**: The `offset` field in `ListFlagRequest`, `ListSegmentRequest`, `ListRuleRequest`, and `ListNamespaceRequest` is deprecated\n- **Deprecated Since**: v1.13.0\n- **Migration Path**:\n  - Replace `offset: <int>` with `page_token: <string>`\n  - Store and use the `next_page_token` from responses for pagination\n  - Example REST call:\n    ```bash\n    # Old (offset-based)\n    GET /api/v1/flags?limit=10&offset=20\n\n    # New (cursor-based)\n    GET /api/v1/flags?limit=10&page_token=abc123xyz\n    ```\n  - Continue requesting with the `next_page_token` until empty\n\n### **EvaluationResponse**: Single segment_key replaced with segment_keys array\n\n- **Component**: `flipt.EvaluationResponse` message (gRPC proto)\n- **Impact**: Field `segment_key` (field #6) is deprecated in favor of `segment_keys` (field #13)\n- **Reason**: Support for segment ANDing/ORing in rules and rollouts requires multiple segment support\n- **Migration Path**:\n  - Change from: `response.segment_key` → `response.segment_keys[0]` (first element)\n  - If you need all matching segments: iterate `response.segment_keys` array\n  - The `segment_key` field will still be populated with the first segment for backward compatibility during deprecation period\n\n### **Rule/Rollout Segment Specification**: Single segment_key replaced with array-based specification\n\n- **Component**: `flipt.Rule.segment_key` and `flipt.RolloutSegment.segment_key` (proto)\n- **Impact**: Rules and rollouts must now specify segments as arrays with an operator\n- **Migration Path**:\n  ```protobuf\n  # Old (Rule)\n  message Rule {\n    string segment_key = 2; // ❌ deprecated\n  }\n\n  # New (Rule)\n  message Rule {\n    repeated string segment_keys = 7;\n    SegmentOperator segment_operator = 8; // OR (0) or AND (1)\n  }\n  ```\n  - For REST API, use new fields in request/response bodies\n  - If migrating from single segment to multiple: set `segment_keys = [old_segment_key]` with operator `OR`\n\n### **gRPC Evaluate/BatchEvaluate Methods**: Deprecated in favor of EvaluationService\n\n- **Component**: `flipt.Flipt.Evaluate()` and `flipt.Flipt.BatchEvaluate()` RPC methods\n- **Impact**: These methods are deprecated and marked for removal\n- **Recommended Replacement**: Use `flipt.evaluation.EvaluationService`:\n  ```protobuf\n  // Old (Flipt service)\n  service Flipt {\n    rpc Evaluate(EvaluationRequest) returns (EvaluationResponse); // ❌ deprecated\n    rpc BatchEvaluate(BatchEvaluationRequest) returns (BatchEvaluationResponse); // ❌ deprecated\n  }\n\n  // New (EvaluationService)\n  service EvaluationService {\n    rpc Boolean(EvaluationRequest) returns (BooleanEvaluationResponse);\n    rpc Variant(EvaluationRequest) returns (VariantEvaluationResponse);\n    rpc Batch(BatchEvaluationRequest) returns (BatchEvaluationResponse);\n  }\n  ```\n  - The new service provides type-safe responses per flag type\n  - All gRPC clients should migrate to EvaluationService\n\n### **Jaeger Tracing Exporter**: Removed in v1.36.0\n\n- **Component**: Tracing configuration\n- **Impact**: Configuration option `tracing.jaeger.*` no longer supported\n- **Reason**: OpenTelemetry officially dropped support for Jaeger exporter in July 2023\n- **Migration Path**:\n  ```yaml\n  # Old (.flipt.yaml) - ❌ No longer works\n  tracing:\n    jaeger:\n      enabled: true\n      host: localhost\n      port: 6831\n\n  # New - Use OTLP exporter instead\n  tracing:\n    exporter: otlp\n    otlp:\n      endpoint: localhost:4317\n  ```\n\n## New Features\n\n### **OpenTelemetry Tracing Enhancements** (Latest)\n\n- **Component**: Tracing configuration and instrumentation\n- **Features Added**:\n  - **Sampling Ratio**: New `tracing.samplingRatio` configuration option for trace sampling control\n    ```yaml\n    tracing:\n      samplingRatio: 0.1  # Sample 10% of traces\n    ```\n  - **Custom Propagators**: New `tracing.propagators` configuration for distributed tracing context propagation\n    ```yaml\n    tracing:\n      propagators:\n        - jaeger\n        - b3\n        - w3c\n    ```\n  - **Feature Flag Semantics**: Added OpenTelemetry semantic conventions for feature flag operations\n    - Automatically includes `feature_flag.key`, `feature_flag.variant`, `feature_flag.enabled` in trace attributes\n\n### **Entity ID Constraint Type** (v1.38.0)\n\n- **Component**: Constraints API\n- **Feature**: New constraint comparison type `ENTITY_ID_COMPARISON_TYPE` for entity identity matching\n- **API Endpoint**: `POST /api/v1/namespaces/{namespace}/segments/{segment}/constraints`\n- **Proto Message**: `flipt.Constraint` with new `comparison_type` enum value\n- **Use Case**: Match flags/segments based on entity ID patterns or values\n- **Example**:\n  ```json\n  {\n    \"type\": \"STRING_COMPARISON_TYPE\",\n    \"operator\": \"EQ\",\n    \"property\": \"entity_id\",\n    \"value\": \"user-123\"\n  }\n  ```\n\n### **Segment ANDing/ORing** (v1.25.0)\n\n- **Component**: Rules and Rollouts\n- **Feature**: Multiple segments can now be combined with AND/OR logic in rules and rollouts\n- **New Fields**:\n  - `segment_keys` (array) - replaces single `segment_key`\n  - `segment_operator` (enum) - `OR` (0) or `AND` (1)\n- **Proto**: Updated `flipt.Rule` and `flipt.RolloutSegment` messages\n- **Example Scenario**:\n  - Rule applies if segment A AND segment B match (operator = AND)\n  - Rollout targets if segment X OR segment Y (operator = OR)\n\n### **Boolean Flag Type** (v1.24.0)\n\n- **Component**: Flag API\n- **Feature**: New flag type `BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE` for boolean on/off feature flags\n- **Proto**: New `FlagType` enum value\n- **Dedicated Evaluation Endpoint**:\n  - New: `flipt.evaluation.EvaluationService.Boolean()` RPC method\n  - REST: `POST /api/v1/evaluate/boolean` endpoint\n- **Response**: `BooleanEvaluationResponse` with `enabled` field instead of `value`\n- **Use Case**: Simple feature toggles that don't require variants\n\n### **Namespaced Authentication Tokens** (v1.31.0)\n\n- **Component**: Authentication API\n- **Feature**: Auth tokens can now be scoped to specific namespaces\n- **Benefit**: Fine-grained access control - tokens limited to particular environments/namespaces\n- **Proto**: `flipt.auth.AuthenticationMethodToken` extended with optional `namespace_keys` field\n- **Example Use**: Token for CI/CD pipeline scoped only to \"production\" namespace\n\n### **JWT Authentication Method** (v1.35.0)\n\n- **Component**: Authentication API\n- **Feature**: New authentication method supporting JWT tokens\n- **Proto Service**: `flipt.auth.AuthenticationMethodJWT`\n- **Configuration**: Set `authentication.method: jwt` with OIDC discovery endpoint\n- **Use Case**: Integrate with existing JWT-based identity providers (Auth0, Okta, etc.)\n\n### **New Storage Backends**\n\n- **Google Cloud Storage (GCS)** (v1.35.0+): Filesystem operations backed by GCS buckets\n- **Azure Blob Storage** (v1.34.0+): FS object backend for Azure deployments\n- **S3 Filesystem Backend** (v1.24.0+): S3-backed filesystem operations\n- **OCI Container Registry** (v1.31.0+): Store feature flag snapshots in OCI registries with AWS ECR improvements (v1.40.0)\n\n### **Server Version Checking** (v1.38.0)\n\n- **Component**: Metadata API\n- **Feature**: New capability to check Flipt server version\n- **Endpoint**: `GET /api/v1/meta/info` (REST) or `MetadataService.GetInfo()` (gRPC)\n- **Use Case**: Clients can verify server compatibility before making advanced API calls\n\n### **Git Storage Directory Scope** (v1.40.0)\n\n- **Component**: Git filesystem backend\n- **Feature**: `flipt validate` command now accepts working directory parameter\n- **Configuration**: New `fs.git.directory` config option to scope git operations to subdirectory\n- **Use Case**: Point Flipt to specific directory within a git repository\n\n### **Rollout Descriptions** (v1.31.0)\n\n- **Component**: Rollout API\n- **Feature**: Optional `description` field added to `flipt.Rollout` message\n- **Use Case**: Document rollout purpose and strategy\n\n## Deprecations\n\n### **Single Segment Key in Rules** (since v1.25.0)\n\n- **Deprecated Field**: `flipt.Rule.segment_key`\n- **Replacement**: `flipt.Rule.segment_keys` (array) with `flipt.Rule.segment_operator`\n- **Removal Timeline**: ~1 year from v1.25.0 release\n- **Migration Note**: Backward compatibility maintained - single `segment_key` auto-converts to array\n\n### **Single Segment Key in Rollout Segments** (since v1.25.0)\n\n- **Deprecated Field**: `flipt.RolloutSegment.segment_key`\n- **Replacement**: `flipt.RolloutSegment.segment_keys` (array) with `flipt.RolloutSegment.segment_operator`\n- **Removal Timeline**: ~1 year from v1.25.0 release\n\n### **Offset-Based Pagination** (since v1.13.0)\n\n- **Deprecated Field**: `offset` in List*Request messages (all services)\n- **Replacement**: `page_token` and `next_page_token` for cursor-based pagination\n- **Removal Timeline**: ~1 year from v1.13.0 release\n- **Status**: Long-standing deprecation; strongly recommend migration\n\n### **Singular segment_key in EvaluationResponse** (since v1.25.0)\n\n- **Deprecated Field**: `flipt.EvaluationResponse.segment_key`\n- **Replacement**: `flipt.EvaluationResponse.segment_keys` (array)\n- **Reason**: Multiple segments can now match evaluation\n- **Removal Timeline**: ~1 year from v1.25.0 release\n- **Note**: Still populated for backward compatibility\n\n### **Old Evaluate/BatchEvaluate Methods** (since v1.29.0)\n\n- **Deprecated Methods**: `flipt.Flipt.Evaluate()` and `flipt.Flipt.BatchEvaluate()`\n- **Replacement**: Use `flipt.evaluation.EvaluationService` with type-safe methods\n- **Removal Timeline**: ~1 year from deprecation\n- **Benefits of Migration**: Type-safe responses, separate endpoints for boolean vs variant evaluation\n\n### **authentication.exclude.metadata** Configuration (since v1.37.0)\n\n- **Deprecated Setting**: `authentication.exclude.metadata` in YAML config\n- **Reason**: Better metadata handling built into authentication methods\n- **Timeline**: Monitor official Flipt docs for removal date\n- **Migration**: Review authentication method configuration for metadata control\n\n## Bug Fixes\n\n### **Constraint Operator Logic** (v1.39.2)\n\n- **Component**: Constraint Evaluation\n- **Issue**: `isnotoneof` operator was using incorrect comparison logic\n- **Impact**: Segments using \"is not one of\" constraints were evaluated incorrectly\n- **Fix**: Corrected operator implementation to properly negate membership tests\n\n### **Segment Constraints Across Namespaces** (v1.39.2)\n\n- **Component**: Segment API\n- **Issue**: Constraints on the same segment key in different namespaces were interfering with each other\n- **Impact**: Evaluations in one namespace could be affected by constraints defined in another namespace\n- **Fix**: Isolated namespace scope for constraint resolution\n\n### **JSON Schema Validation for Segment Constraints** (v1.40.0)\n\n- **Component**: Constraint Validation\n- **Issue**: JSON schema validation for `key|keys` properties in rollout segments was rejecting valid inputs\n- **Impact**: Valid rollout segment configurations were failing validation\n- **Fix**: Corrected JSON schema to properly handle array and single-value key specifications\n\n### **Flipt Data API Segment Shadowing** (v1.38.2)\n\n- **Component**: Data API (EvaluationSnapshot)\n- **Issue**: Segment definitions could shadow each other in Data API responses\n- **Impact**: Snapshots returned incorrect segment data when segments had similar keys\n- **Fix**: Implemented proper segment identifier isolation in snapshot generation\n\n### **Authentication Cache Hash Storage** (v1.40.1)\n\n- **Component**: Authentication\n- **Issue**: Full authentication credentials being stored in cache instead of hash\n- **Security Impact**: Reduced exposure of auth credentials in cache layer\n- **Fix**: Only hash values are now cached; full credentials not persisted\n\n### **Database Connection in Auth Layer** (v1.40.1)\n\n- **Component**: Authentication\n- **Issue**: Unnecessary database connections being established when not needed\n- **Impact**: Increased resource usage, slower auth initialization\n- **Fix**: Conditional database connection establishment based on auth configuration\n\n### **Redis Authentication Username** (v1.40.1)\n\n- **Component**: Cache (Redis)\n- **Issue**: Username parameter not accepted in Redis configuration\n- **Impact**: Redis instances requiring authentication couldn't be configured with username\n- **Fix**: Added username field support in redis configuration structure\n\n### **Evaluation Cache Key Handling** (v1.28.2)\n\n- **Component**: Caching Layer\n- **Issue**: Incorrect cache key generation for new evaluation endpoints vs old endpoints\n- **Impact**: Cache misses and inconsistent caching behavior between Flipt and EvaluationService endpoints\n- **Fix**: Unified cache key generation across all evaluation methods\n\n## Upgrade Guide\n\n### Step 1: Review Current API Usage\n\nBefore upgrading, identify how your application uses Flipt:\n\n- Check if you're using `EvaluationService` or the older `Flipt.Evaluate()` methods\n- Identify any List operations in your code (pagination)\n- Note if you're using Jaeger tracing configuration\n- Review any custom segments or rules using multiple segments\n\n### Step 2: Update Configuration Files\n\n1. **If using Jaeger tracing** (pre-v1.36.0):\n   ```yaml\n   # BEFORE (.flipt.yaml)\n   tracing:\n     jaeger:\n       enabled: true\n       host: localhost\n       port: 6831\n\n   # AFTER\n   tracing:\n     exporter: otlp\n     otlp:\n       endpoint: localhost:4317\n   ```\n\n2. **Add new tracing configuration** (optional, v1.38.0+):\n   ```yaml\n   tracing:\n     samplingRatio: 0.1  # Sample 10% for production\n     propagators:\n       - w3c  # or jaeger, b3, etc.\n   ```\n\n3. **Review authentication configuration**:\n   - If using auth, verify `authentication.method` is correctly set\n   - Check for deprecated `authentication.exclude.metadata` and update if present\n\n### Step 3: Update API Clients\n\n#### For gRPC Clients (Recommended)\n\n**Update evaluation calls to use EvaluationService:**\n\n```go\n// OLD (Deprecated, pre-v1.29.0)\nclient.Evaluate(ctx, &flipt.EvaluationRequest{\n    FlagKey:  \"feature-x\",\n    EntityID: \"user-123\",\n})\n\n// NEW (Recommended, v1.29.0+)\n// For variant flags:\nclient.Variant(ctx, &flipt.EvaluationRequest{\n    FlagKey:  \"feature-x\",\n    EntityID: \"user-123\",\n})\n\n// For boolean flags:\nclient.Boolean(ctx, &flipt.EvaluationRequest{\n    FlagKey:  \"feature-x\",\n    EntityID: \"user-123\",\n})\n```\n\n#### For REST API Clients\n\n**Update pagination:**\n\n```bash\n# OLD (offset-based, pre-v1.13.0)\ncurl -X GET \"http://flipt:8080/api/v1/flags?limit=10&offset=20\"\n\n# NEW (cursor-based, v1.13.0+)\n# First request\ncurl -X GET \"http://flipt:8080/api/v1/flags?limit=10\"\n# Response includes: {\"flags\": [...], \"next_page_token\": \"abc123\"}\n\n# Subsequent requests use the token\ncurl -X GET \"http://flipt:8080/api/v1/flags?limit=10&page_token=abc123\"\n```\n\n**Update boolean flag evaluation:**\n\n```bash\n# NEW endpoint (v1.24.0+)\ncurl -X POST \"http://flipt:8080/api/v1/evaluate/boolean\" \\\n  -H \"Content-Type: application/json\" \\\n  -d '{\n    \"flag_key\": \"dark_mode\",\n    \"entity_id\": \"user-123\",\n    \"context\": {}\n  }'\n```\n\n### Step 4: Update Segment/Rule Definitions\n\n**For rules with multiple segments** (if migrating from workarounds):\n\n```json\n// If using new segment ANDing feature (v1.25.0+)\n{\n  \"flag_key\": \"feature-x\",\n  \"segment_keys\": [\"beta-users\", \"us-region\"],\n  \"segment_operator\": \"AND\",  // Match if in both segments\n  \"rank\": 1,\n  \"value\": \"on\"\n}\n```\n\n### Step 5: Run Tests and Validation\n\n1. **Validate configuration**:\n   ```bash\n   flipt validate --config .flipt.yaml\n   ```\n\n2. **Run your application test suite** to verify API compatibility:\n   - Test list pagination endpoints\n   - Test evaluation endpoints\n   - Test rule/segment creation if applicable\n\n3. **Test tracing** (if using OTLP):\n   - Verify traces are being exported to your collector\n   - Check trace attributes for feature flag semantics\n\n### Step 6: Deploy and Monitor\n\n1. **Backup existing data** (especially database if running Flipt with persistent storage)\n\n2. **Deploy new version** in staging first:\n   ```bash\n   docker pull flipt:latest  # or your version\n   docker run -v /path/to/.flipt.yaml:/etc/flipt/.flipt.yaml flipt\n   ```\n\n3. **Monitor logs** for deprecation warnings:\n   - Pagination errors (if clients still use offset)\n   - Auth-related issues\n   - Tracing connection issues\n\n4. **Gradually roll out** to production if managing multiple instances\n\n### Step 7: Post-Upgrade Validation\n\n- Verify all features are evaluating correctly\n- Check dashboard and analytics (if enabled)\n- Monitor performance metrics and tracing data\n- Update team documentation on new API features\n\n### Rollback Plan\n\nIf issues occur:\n\n1. Revert to previous image/binary version\n2. Restore database backup if applicable\n3. Clear any caches that might have incompatible data\n4. Flipt Release Notes\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\n> These changes require action from users upgrading.\n\n### **Pagination API**: Offset-based pagination removed in favor of cursor-based pagination\n\n- **Component**: List operations (flags, segments, rules, namespaces)\n- **Impact**: The `offset` field in `ListFlagRequest`, `ListSegmentRequest`, `ListRuleRequest`, and `ListNamespaceRequest` is deprecated\n- **Deprecated Since**: v1.13.0\n- **Migration Path**:\n  - Replace `offset: <int>` with `page_token: <string>`\n  - Store and use the `next_page_token` from responses for pagination\n  - Example REST call:\n    ```bash\n    # Old (offset-based)\n    GET /api/v1/flags?limit=10&offset=20\n\n    # New (cursor-based)\n    GET /api/v1/flags?limit=10&page_token=abc123xyz\n    ```\n  - Continue requesting with the `next_page_token` until empty\n\n### **EvaluationResponse**: Single segment_key replaced with segment_keys array\n\n- **Component**: `flipt.EvaluationResponse` message (gRPC proto)\n- **Impact**: Field `segment_key` (field #6) is deprecated in favor of `segment_keys` (field #13)\n- **Reason**: Support for segment ANDing/ORing in rules and rollouts requires multiple segment support\n- **Migration Path**:\n  - Change from: `response.segment_key` → `response.segment_keys[0]` (first element)\n  - If you need all matching segments: iterate `response.segment_keys` array\n  - The `segment_key` field will still be populated with the first segment for backward compatibility during deprecation period\n\n### **Rule/Rollout Segment Specification**: Single segment_key replaced with array-based specification\n\n- **Component**: `flipt.Rule.segment_key` and `flipt.RolloutSegment.segment_key` (proto)\n- **Impact**: Rules and rollouts must now specify segments as arrays with an operator\n- **Migration Path**:\n  ```protobuf\n  # Old (Rule)\n  message Rule {\n    string segment_key = 2; // ❌ deprecated\n  }\n\n  # New (Rule)\n  message Rule {\n    repeated string segment_keys = 7;\n    SegmentOperator segment_operator = 8; // OR (0) or AND (1)\n  }\n  ```\n  - For REST API, use new fields in request/response bodies\n  - If migrating from single segment to multiple: set `segment_keys = [old_segment_key]` with operator `OR`\n\n### **gRPC Evaluate/BatchEvaluate Methods**: Deprecated in favor of EvaluationService\n\n- **Component**: `flipt.Flipt.Evaluate()` and `flipt.Flipt.BatchEvaluate()` RPC methods\n- **Impact**: These methods are deprecated and marked for removal\n- **Recommended Replacement**: Use `flipt.evaluation.EvaluationService`:\n  ```protobuf\n  // Old (Flipt service)\n  service Flipt {\n    rpc Evaluate(EvaluationRequest) returns (EvaluationResponse); // ❌ deprecated\n    rpc BatchEvaluate(BatchEvaluationRequest) returns (BatchEvaluationResponse); // ❌ deprecated\n  }\n\n  // New (EvaluationService)\n  service EvaluationService {\n    rpc Boolean(EvaluationRequest) returns (BooleanEvaluationResponse);\n    rpc Variant(EvaluationRequest) returns (VariantEvaluationResponse);\n    rpc Batch(BatchEvaluationRequest) returns (BatchEvaluationResponse);\n  }\n  ```\n  - The new service provides type-safe responses per flag type\n  - All gRPC clients should migrate to EvaluationService\n\n### **Jaeger Tracing Exporter**: Removed in v1.36.0\n\n- **Component**: Tracing configuration\n- **Impact**: Configuration option `tracing.jaeger.*` no longer supported\n- **Reason**: OpenTelemetry officially dropped support for Jaeger exporter in July 2023\n- **Migration Path**:\n  ```yaml\n  # Old (.flipt.yaml) - ❌ No longer works\n  tracing:\n    jaeger:\n      enabled: true\n      host: localhost\n      port: 6831\n\n  # New - Use OTLP exporter instead\n  tracing:\n    exporter: otlp\n    otlp:\n      endpoint: localhost:4317\n  ```\n\n## New Features\n\n### **OpenTelemetry Tracing Enhancements** (Latest)\n\n- **Component**: Tracing configuration and instrumentation\n- **Features Added**:\n  - **Sampling Ratio**: New `tracing.samplingRatio` configuration option for trace sampling control\n    ```yaml\n    tracing:\n      samplingRatio: 0.1  # Sample 10% of traces\n    ```\n  - **Custom Propagators**: New `tracing.propagators` configuration for distributed tracing context propagation\n    ```yaml\n    tracing:\n      propagators:\n        - jaeger\n        - b3\n        - w3c\n    ```\n  - **Feature Flag Semantics**: Added OpenTelemetry semantic conventions for feature flag operations\n    - Automatically includes `feature_flag.key`, `feature_flag.variant`, `feature_flag.enabled` in trace attributes\n\n### **Entity ID Constraint Type** (v1.38.0)\n\n- **Component**: Constraints API\n- **Feature**: New constraint comparison type `ENTITY_ID_COMPARISON_TYPE` for entity identity matching\n- **API Endpoint**: `POST /api/v1/namespaces/{namespace}/segments/{segment}/constraints`\n- **Proto Message**: `flipt.Constraint` with new `comparison_type` enum value\n- **Use Case**: Match flags/segments based on entity ID patterns or values\n- **Example**:\n  ```json\n  {\n    \"type\": \"STRING_COMPARISON_TYPE\",\n    \"operator\": \"EQ\",\n    \"property\": \"entity_id\",\n    \"value\": \"user-123\"\n  }\n  ```\n\n### **Segment ANDing/ORing** (v1.25.0)\n\n- **Component**: Rules and Rollouts\n- **Feature**: Multiple segments can now be combined with AND/OR logic in rules and rollouts\n- **New Fields**:\n  - `segment_keys` (array) - replaces single `segment_key`\n  - `segment_operator` (enum) - `OR` (0) or `AND` (1)\n- **Proto**: Updated `flipt.Rule` and `flipt.RolloutSegment` messages\n- **Example Scenario**:\n  - Rule applies if segment A AND segment B match (operator = AND)\n  - Rollout targets if segment X OR segment Y (operator = OR)\n\n### **Boolean Flag Type** (v1.24.0)\n\n- **Component**: Flag API\n- **Feature**: New flag type `BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE` for boolean on/off feature flags\n- **Proto**: New `FlagType` enum value\n- **Dedicated Evaluation Endpoint**:\n  - New: `flipt.evaluation.EvaluationService.Boolean()` RPC method\n  - REST: `POST /api/v1/evaluate/boolean` endpoint\n- **Response**: `BooleanEvaluationResponse` with `enabled` field instead of `value`\n- **Use Case**: Simple feature toggles that don't require variants\n\n### **Namespaced Authentication Tokens** (v1.31.0)\n\n- **Component**: Authentication API\n- **Feature**: Auth tokens can now be scoped to specific namespaces\n- **Benefit**: Fine-grained access control - tokens limited to particular environments/namespaces\n- **Proto**: `flipt.auth.AuthenticationMethodToken` extended with optional `namespace_keys` field\n- **Example Use**: Token for CI/CD pipeline scoped only to \"production\" namespace\n\n### **JWT Authentication Method** (v1.35.0)\n\n- **Component**: Authentication API\n- **Feature**: New authentication method supporting JWT tokens\n- **Proto Service**: `flipt.auth.AuthenticationMethodJWT`\n- **Configuration**: Set `authentication.method: jwt` with OIDC discovery endpoint\n- **Use Case**: Integrate with existing JWT-based identity providers (Auth0, Okta, etc.)\n\n### **New Storage Backends**\n\n- **Google Cloud Storage (GCS)** (v1.35.0+): Filesystem operations backed by GCS buckets\n- **Azure Blob Storage** (v1.34.0+): FS object backend for Azure deployments\n- **S3 Filesystem Backend** (v1.24.0+): S3-backed filesystem operations\n- **OCI Container Registry** (v1.31.0+): Store feature flag snapshots in OCI registries with AWS ECR improvements (v1.40.0)\n\n### **Server Version Checking** (v1.38.0)\n\n- **Component**: Metadata API\n- **Feature**: New capability to check Flipt server version\n- **Endpoint**: `GET /api/v1/meta/info` (REST) or `MetadataService.GetInfo()` (gRPC)\n- **Use Case**: Clients can verify server compatibility before making advanced API calls\n\n### **Git Storage Directory Scope** (v1.40.0)\n\n- **Component**: Git filesystem backend\n- **Feature**: `flipt validate` command now accepts working directory parameter\n- **Configuration**: New `fs.git.directory` config option to scope git operations to subdirectory\n- **Use Case**: Point Flipt to specific directory within a git repository\n\n### **Rollout Descriptions** (v1.31.0)\n\n- **Component**: Rollout API\n- **Feature**: Optional `description` field added to `flipt.Rollout` message\n- **Use Case**: Document rollout purpose and strategy\n\n## Deprecations\n\n### **Single Segment Key in Rules** (since v1.25.0)\n\n- **Deprecated Field**: `flipt.Rule.segment_key`\n- **Replacement**: `flipt.Rule.segment_keys` (array) with `flipt.Rule.segment_operator`\n- **Removal Timeline**: ~1 year from v1.25.0 release\n- **Migration Note**: Backward compatibility maintained - single `segment_key` auto-converts to array\n\n### **Single Segment Key in Rollout Segments** (since v1.25.0)\n\n- **Deprecated Field**: `flipt.RolloutSegment.segment_key`\n- **Replacement**: `flipt.RolloutSegment.segment_keys` (array) with `flipt.RolloutSegment.segment_operator`\n- **Removal Timeline**: ~1 year from v1.25.0 release\n\n### **Offset-Based Pagination** (since v1.13.0)\n\n- **Deprecated Field**: `offset` in List*Request messages (all services)\n- **Replacement**: `page_token` and `next_page_token` for cursor-based pagination\n- **Removal Timeline**: ~1 year from v1.13.0 release\n- **Status**: Long-standing deprecation; strongly recommend migration\n\n### **Singular segment_key in EvaluationResponse** (since v1.25.0)\n\n- **Deprecated Field**: `flipt.EvaluationResponse.segment_key`\n- **Replacement**: `flipt.EvaluationResponse.segment_keys` (array)\n- **Reason**: Multiple segments can now match evaluation\n- **Removal Timeline**: ~1 year from v1.25.0 release\n- **Note**: Still populated for backward compatibility\n\n### **Old Evaluate/BatchEvaluate Methods** (since v1.29.0)\n\n- **Deprecated Methods**: `flipt.Flipt.Evaluate()` and `flipt.Flipt.BatchEvaluate()`\n- **Replacement**: Use `flipt.evaluation.EvaluationService` with type-safe methods\n- **Removal Timeline**: ~1 year from deprecation\n- **Benefits of Migration**: Type-safe responses, separate endpoints for boolean vs variant evaluation\n\n### **authentication.exclude.metadata** Configuration (since v1.37.0)\n\n- **Deprecated Setting**: `authentication.exclude.metadata` in YAML config\n- **Reason**: Better metadata handling built into authentication methods\n- **Timeline**: Monitor official Flipt docs for removal date\n- **Migration**: Review authentication method configuration for metadata control\n\n## Bug Fixes\n\n### **Constraint Operator Logic** (v1.39.2)\n\n- **Component**: Constraint Evaluation\n- **Issue**: `isnotoneof` operator was using incorrect comparison logic\n- **Impact**: Segments using \"is not one of\" constraints were evaluated incorrectly\n- **Fix**: Corrected operator implementation to properly negate membership tests\n\n### **Segment Constraints Across Namespaces** (v1.39.2)\n\n- **Component**: Segment API\n- **Issue**: Constraints on the same segment key in different namespaces were interfering with each other\n- **Impact**: Evaluations in one namespace could be affected by constraints defined in another namespace\n- **Fix**: Isolated namespace scope for constraint resolution\n\n### **JSON Schema Validation for Segment Constraints** (v1.40.0)\n\n- **Component**: Constraint Validation\n- **Issue**: JSON schema validation for `key|keys` properties in rollout segments was rejecting valid inputs\n- **Impact**: Valid rollout segment configurations were failing validation\n- **Fix**: Corrected JSON schema to properly handle array and single-value key specifications\n\n### **Flipt Data API Segment Shadowing** (v1.38.2)\n\n- **Component**: Data API (EvaluationSnapshot)\n- **Issue**: Segment definitions could shadow each other in Data API responses\n- **Impact**: Snapshots returned incorrect segment data when segments had similar keys\n- **Fix**: Implemented proper segment identifier isolation in snapshot generation\n\n### **Authentication Cache Hash Storage** (v1.40.1)\n\n- **Component**: Authentication\n- **Issue**: Full authentication credentials being stored in cache instead of hash\n- **Security Impact**: Reduced exposure of auth credentials in cache layer\n- **Fix**: Only hash values are now cached; full credentials not persisted\n\n### **Database Connection in Auth Layer** (v1.40.1)\n\n- **Component**: Authentication\n- **Issue**: Unnecessary database connections being established when not needed\n- **Impact**: Increased resource usage, slower auth initialization\n- **Fix**: Conditional database connection establishment based on auth configuration\n\n### **Redis Authentication Username** (v1.40.1)\n\n- **Component**: Cache (Redis)\n- **Issue**: Username parameter not accepted in Redis configuration\n- **Impact**: Redis instances requiring authentication couldn't be configured with username\n- **Fix**: Added username field support in redis configuration structure\n\n### **Evaluation Cache Key Handling** (v1.28.2)\n\n- **Component**: Caching Layer\n- **Issue**: Incorrect cache key generation for new evaluation endpoints vs old endpoints\n- **Impact**: Cache misses and inconsistent caching behavior between Flipt and EvaluationService endpoints\n- **Fix**: Unified cache key generation across all evaluation methods\n\n## Upgrade Guide\n\n### Step 1: Review Current API Usage\n\nBefore upgrading, identify how your application uses Flipt:\n\n- Check if you're using `EvaluationService` or the older `Flipt.Evaluate()` methods\n- Identify any List operations in your code (pagination)\n- Note if you're using Jaeger tracing configuration\n- Review any custom segments or rules using multiple segments\n\n### Step 2: Update Configuration Files\n\n1. **If using Jaeger tracing** (pre-v1.36.0):\n   ```yaml\n   # BEFORE (.flipt.yaml)\n   tracing:\n     jaeger:\n       enabled: true\n       host: localhost\n       port: 6831\n\n   # AFTER\n   tracing:\n     exporter: otlp\n     otlp:\n       endpoint: localhost:4317\n   ```\n\n2. **Add new tracing configuration** (optional, v1.38.0+):\n   ```yaml\n   tracing:\n     samplingRatio: 0.1  # Sample 10% for production\n     propagators:\n       - w3c  # or jaeger, b3, etc.\n   ```\n\n3. **Review authentication configuration**:\n   - If using auth, verify `authentication.method` is correctly set\n   - Check for deprecated `authentication.exclude.metadata` and update if present\n\n### Step 3: Update API Clients\n\n#### For gRPC Clients (Recommended)\n\n**Update evaluation calls to use EvaluationService:**\n\n```go\n// OLD (Deprecated, pre-v1.29.0)\nclient.Evaluate(ctx, &flipt.EvaluationRequest{\n    FlagKey:  \"feature-x\",\n    EntityID: \"user-123\",\n})\n\n// NEW (Recommended, v1.29.0+)\n// For variant flags:\nclient.Variant(ctx, &flipt.EvaluationRequest{\n    FlagKey:  \"feature-x\",\n    EntityID: \"user-123\",\n})\n\n// For boolean flags:\nclient.Boolean(ctx, &flipt.EvaluationRequest{\n    FlagKey:  \"feature-x\",\n    EntityID: \"user-123\",\n})\n```\n\n#### For REST API Clients\n\n**Update pagination:**\n\n```bash\n# OLD (offset-based, pre-v1.13.0)\ncurl -X GET \"http://flipt:8080/api/v1/flags?limit=10&offset=20\"\n\n# NEW (cursor-based, v1.13.0+)\n# First request\ncurl -X GET \"http://flipt:8080/api/v1/flags?limit=10\"\n# Response includes: {\"flags\": [...], \"next_page_token\": \"abc123\"}\n\n# Subsequent requests use the token\ncurl -X GET \"http://flipt:8080/api/v1/flags?limit=10&page_token=abc123\"\n```\n\n**Update boolean flag evaluation:**\n\n```bash\n# NEW endpoint (v1.24.0+)\ncurl -X POST \"http://flipt:8080/api/v1/evaluate/boolean\" \\\n  -H \"Content-Type: application/json\" \\\n  -d '{\n    \"flag_key\": \"dark_mode\",\n    \"entity_id\": \"user-123\",\n    \"context\": {}\n  }'\n```\n\n### Step 4: Update Segment/Rule Definitions\n\n**For rules with multiple segments** (if migrating from workarounds):\n\n```json\n// If using new segment ANDing feature (v1.25.0+)\n{\n  \"flag_key\": \"feature-x\",\n  \"segment_keys\": [\"beta-users\", \"us-region\"],\n  \"segment_operator\": \"AND\",  // Match if in both segments\n  \"rank\": 1,\n  \"value\": \"on\"\n}\n```\n\n### Step 5: Run Tests and Validation\n\n1. **Validate configuration**:\n   ```bash\n   flipt validate --config .flipt.yaml\n   ```\n\n2. **Run your application test suite** to verify API compatibility:\n   - Test list pagination endpoints\n   - Test evaluation endpoints\n   - Test rule/segment creation if applicable\n\n3. **Test tracing** (if using OTLP):\n   - Verify traces are being exported to your collector\n   - Check trace attributes for feature flag semantics\n\n### Step 6: Deploy and Monitor\n\n1. **Backup existing data** (especially database if running Flipt with persistent storage)\n\n2. **Deploy new version** in staging first:\n   ```bash\n   docker pull flipt:latest  # or your version\n   docker run -v /path/to/.flipt.yaml:/etc/flipt/.flipt.yaml flipt\n   ```\n\n3. **Monitor logs** for deprecation warnings:\n   - Pagination errors (if clients still use offset)\n   - Auth-related issues\n   - Tracing connection issues\n\n4. **Gradually roll out** to production if managing multiple instances\n\n### Step 7: Post-Upgrade Validation\n\n- Verify all features are evaluating correctly\n- Check dashboard and analytics (if enabled)\n- Monitor performance metrics and tracing data\n- Update team documentation on new API features\n\n### Rollback Plan\n\nIf issues occur:\n\n1. Revert to previous image/binary version\n2. Restore database backup if applicable\n3. Clear any caches that might have incompatible data\n4.
